You may not back out of sales or will be removed. Please delete items immediately if you cross post and sell on another site. Sellers must respond to deal questions within 12 hours.                <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 FashionSTYLE Magazine
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 fashionSTYLE was described by a blogger as “the region’s most powerful social tool for reaching the serious fashionista!” Their wide-reaching influence stems from various sources, including the persona and achievements of its most famous editor and publisher, Lamont and Jeana Bowling. Often described as the “Fashion Power Couple” their various charitable and community projects, their pure love for the fashion industry and their ability to pioneer into the industry has placed them amongst the who’s who in the Philadelphia, New Jersey fashion scene. fashionSTYLE Magazine was created as an industry publication in 2005 with the concept of bringing high end fashion reports to retailers that served a younger consumer. “There is a community of young people, ages 18 – 25 that don’t always wear baggy jeans and boots, leggins and a big sweater. There are young people that like to look elegant. That likes to dress before they go out.” “The 18 – 25 year olds are our largest consumers in the retail clothing industry, let’s give them more options than collegiate sweaters and fitted baseball caps.” During the next few years, fashionSTYLE transitioned away from an industry print publication into an online publication that directly served its younger readers. The magazine now included articles on style, fashion events, casting calls, hair and makeup preparation and celebrity blogging. fashionSTYLEmagazine.net’s quick transition immediately opened doors and introduce its pages to a world wide audience. fashionSTYLE Magazine has been sponsors in several fashion events that include Virgin Island Fashion Week, regional fashion networking events, designer trunk shows, the PINK fashion Show and the first ever fashion week and Fashion’s Night Out to Atlantic City. Atlantic City Fashion Week is now a staple in the New York, New Jersey, Philadelphia region with shows in September and in February. Through our sponsored fashion events, direct web site and social media, fashionSTYLEmagazine.net global market numbers in the hundreds of thousands. fashionSTYLE also uses its industry clout for good causes, including toy drives, help for the homeless and it’s most notable, PINK fashion Show which raises awareness to breast cancer. The future for fashionSTYLEmagazine is endless! We will continue to announce, produce and sponsor fashion events that will take our readers to every end of the world. We are always looking for young innovation and creativity. The world is our runway… To contact us at fashionSTYLE Magazine or to get more information about our events go to www.fashionSTYLEmagazine.net www.AtlanticCityFashionWeek.com www.ReadyToWearFashionWeek.com www.sohoFW.com

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Boys only name brand resale BST group with MINIMAL rules!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 We try to have minimal rules but we do want to follow B/S/T ETIQUETTE: ISO only allowed on weekends. All ISO must be deleted by Sunday at midnight or you will be MUTED for 48 hours. PLEASE DELETE your ISO. SELLERS: ALLOWED...BOYS CLOTHING, SHOES, ACCESSORIES SUCH AS BELTS, HATS AND BLANKETS, SWADDLES. ALLOWED: Small Shop items in purges which contain 75% brand name and 25% small shop . NOT ALLOWED ...LINKS ...ONLY LINKS ALLOWED ARE THOSE APPROVED BY JANINE PHILLIPS FISHER.....NO links to shops, stores, BST pages, FB pages, . NO Links posted on page or in PM...if you receive a link..PLEASE CONTACT ME . Regina Phillips NOT ALLOWED ....ISO of Small Shop or party goods or toys . No China brands such as ALI or WISH items. NO Items in bulk. . No Links of any kind. Small shop , instashop, Etsy shop or business owners using the site as a storefront. No Gifting of money. No Asking for PAYPAL fees . No DRAMA.. no price shaming . No live shopping. Posts must include brand, size, condition, price, shipping info, smoke free/pet free. Items that do not state brand, condition and size are subject to removal. Must disclose stains or flaws. YOU MUST USE ACTUAL PICTURES OF THE ITEMS - NO STOCK PHOTOS. 🚫 No claiming items from the main post - claims must be made on each individual picture to make it fair for everyone. ✅ Be familiar with the rules for buyers and make sure you are invoicing the buyer that claimed correctly. You must invoice within 24 hours or the buyer has the right to pass. We advise sellers to use reply feature and that buyers claim the items in Reply to avoid confusion. Holds or questions must still have paypal, and seller should only accept claims with paypal or "will pm paypal" on each item. ✅ Keep up with your purge! Please continue once you start the purge or update and let sellers know what time you will start. ✅ Deal or No Deal (DOND) is allowed, however once you accept an offer you must honor it and cannot then go back and accept higher offers. ✅ If you have a non-payer tag them in your purge AND pm or send PayPal reminder before reaching out to Admin. Not everyone sees the notifications so send a pm to the buyer. ✅ Items must be shipped within 5️⃣ business days. ✅ If you have cross posted items in your purge, please make that clear on your post. ✅ If you are offering an item on someone's ISO post, you may move to next in line after 2 hours, if no one commented . BUYERS: ✅ 😳THE ABSOLUTE ONLY WAY TO SECURE AN ITEM-- post your paypal on the item or items you want. ....or you can state ...”sold will pm PayPal”..If you have a question about an item, you must still post your PayPal and then post your question IMMEDIATELY after. You can then decide if you want to pass. 🚫 DELETING YOUR COMMENT AFTER POSTING PAYPAL IS GROUNDS FOR IMMEDIATE REMOVAL. So is backing out of a sale. If you post your PayPal or will pm PayPal, the item is yours, no exceptions. Make sure you read description, size, price, shipping, etc. before you claim
                </div>

To make sure this group maintains the boutique feel we love, most items are limited quantity and typically two size runs per piece. if you love it, comment before it's gone!! We promise to ship items out as quickly as possible!! If you need an item by a certain date please send us a message and we wills what we can do. Otherwise we ship most items in 7-10 business days!! sometimes quicker and sometimes depending on our vendor it may be longer we try to keep you in the loop if it will take longer, sometimes things are out of our control on vendor shipping times. If you complete your purchase within 1 hour of placing it in your cart your shipping is FREE! In the event that we do a pre-order item the approximate ship date will be posted. however these dates are subject to change depending on the vendors speed of shipping, which is completely out of our control!! How do I contact you? kesoulboutique@gmail.com Emails will be answered Monday-Friday 8am-3pm CST. What payment options to we offer? At this time we accept PayPal and Stripe processing for all cards Can I return an item I have purchased? Returns are only accepted on a damaged item. We will do our best to inspect our inventory before shipping but please inspect your order as soon as it arrives. In the rare case that an item is defective, please notify us via email within 3 business days at kesoulboutique@gmail.com store credit will be issued if a replacement isn't available. if you would like to buy*sell*trade an item, please do so on the K.E Soul BST group page. How do I order? Simply comment under the photo of the item you like with "sold (and your size)" you will be promoted to pay for your item via the program called commentSold. K.E. Soul STL: https://kesoulstl.commentsold.com K.E. Soul MT: https://kesoulmt.commentsold.com

                 Seller: Items posted for bid must start at $1 (plus shipping - please be reasonable with shipping cost! The auction ends on the second before your posted end time. (For example if you select 9AM for your end time the last bid that counts must be posted by 8:59.59!) - All items valued at $100 or more need to have a photo that includes name and date. These packages must be shipped with full insurance! - Bumping is only allowed four times per day, except on the day your auction ends. On that day, you are allowed six bumps to your item. - Items must be shipped in a timely manner, tracking must be updated in PP and diapers must be recieved in the condition you listed! - Fair shipping is required. You may not make money on shipping! If a buyer wins multiple items, you MUST combine shipping. - Do NOT delete your post. - Once your item has been paid for, please mark it as sold. Once the buyer has noted that they received the item, tag an admin or moderator to delete the post! Buyers: - Once you have bid on an item you may not remove your bid! Please ask any questions you have and be PayPal ready before placing a bid. You will have 24hrs to pay your invoice. If you do not pay for an item you've won, you will be removed from the group! - Comment received on seller's post once the auction item is in your possession so admins can delete post. * Interest posts are to be placed in the albums. No interest posts to the wall will be approved! * All Transactions must be paid through PayPal and tracking must be updated in PayPal. Tracking is required for all transactions! *If you're from out of country please state as such and make arrangements for shipping with buyer/seller. *Choosing not to follow any of the rules will result in being banned from the group! *Being brought up in the scam group will result in you being removed from the group! *This is a drama free zone! Please pm an admin if you have an issue. *No Auction Posts may be deleted until buyer receives diaper and admin approves!!                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Thrifting Divas
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 BCBG, Michael Kors, Diane von Furstenberg.... we all love them and lust having them. However, who wants to always pay top dollar to wear them? Thrifting Divas started by Ayana Pitterson, is a group of budget conscious fashionistas dedicated to having the fashion we desire, without breaking our bank accounts to acquire them. We peruse the racks of local thrift shops and second hand stores for the high end fashion that makes us what we are - thrifting divas! This group is open for those who come close to the T word-- "thriftaholics." It's open to that diva who is a newbie in the thrifting world. It's even open to that diva who cannot understand what is to be gained by even entering these sorts of thrift establishment. In this group, all fashionistas are welcomed, but the goal is to understand how thrifting can be incorporated into our daily looks. Work It Wedneday is the only day of the week to post/advertise in the group. Please post once per Wednesday with one picture accompanied by the relevant information. Post, hit like, comment on all things THRIFTING and SAVING!!!!

                 Aloha Fused Hawaii Family, The stories of our growing community have so inspired us. As we build ourselves alongside our brand, we had no idea how powerful the process would be. We want to bring our community together to create a safe space for us to share our stories in hopes to empower others to share theirs as well. Always Roxelle + Team Fused Hawaii SHOP our swimwear in the link below: www.fusedhawaii.com ---------------------------------- GUIDELINES FOR USE ---------------------------------- If you have a promotion for your business or something to sell, please do NOT post it in this group. Posts that seem inappropriate, negative, complaining, blaming, “sob-story telling,” self-victimizing, or self-promoting will be deleted. This is a negativity-free zone and we are happy to keep it that way! :) Please note that this group is NOT to serve as a Fused Hawaii support center. Please address all questions relating to your specific orders to our support team at support@fusedhawaii.com. All questions regarding shipments or delivery times will be deleted to make the most use of Roxelle and her team's time to provide the most value to this group. **NOTE: Trade/ Buy and sell albums are customer-created content. Fused Hawaii is not responsible for any transactions that may take place in the albums section. We recommend doing your due diligence before proceeding with any unsecured transactions within this group. We do not advise doing any transaction outside of this platform and you are 100% responsible for the risk taken when doing so. Our moderators are taking the time weekly to monitor and clean out the albums as a FREE service to our members to enjoy. Please be kind to them as this is an optional service provided by this group to add a fun experience for our community. Also, We ask that you spread as much positivity as you can via comments and likes in each post. We as women at times overlook the need for compliments. Let's encourage a free flow of compliments, and uplifting support as much as possible. If you think something good, Share it! Above all, BE KIND. There's never too much of that in the world.

                 This group is for posting and finding out about lolita clothing and accessory releases and news. This group inspired by the newslolita community that once existed on LJ. Hopefully it will be a place where we all can share information and opinions about the newest lolita releases and meet some cool people! Our group banner was made by Yanyu. Please check her artwork out here: http://scribble-yu.blogspot.com/ How to use Taobao for lolita: https://docs.google.com/document/d/1A0o7bR-WwICp15vmbMKd_nf4KAgWudcroxN2-rYRSp8/pub Rules: NO QUESTIONS - only (objectively if possible) report news you found about the lolita world. If you have a question, either find the thread about the item you have a question about or you can ask it in Lolita Updates' sister group, Rufflechat. https://www.facebook.com/groups/rufflechat/ ♪ You may post news from Japanese lolita or otome brands, indie brands from any country, or taobao brands. ♪ Before you make a new post, please scroll down or use the search function to make sure it hasn't been posted about already. ♪ Only one thread for a release. If your news is an update about something that has already been posted, bump the old thread on the topic instead of making a new one. ♪ You may post about release dates, upcoming events held by lolita brands, lucky packs, sales, novelties, and other relevant information that you think people would be interested in. ♪ If you run an indie brand of clothing or accessories, you may self promote within reason, i.e. post once about your upcoming release but no purposeless bumping. Please contact a moderator to get an okay first! ♪ No promoting of personal tea parties, personal events, sales posts or other groups or communities. You may post about large lolita conventions or official or indie brand international events, but no personal plans for meetups please. ♪ If you want to advertise your new FB group, you must ask permission first. ♪ Resellers and shopping services are not permitted to post about their newly stocked items since it isn't original and not "news". You may, however, introduce your shop once. Contact a moderator first to get an okay. ♪ In keeping with EGL policy, please do not post about replicas here. ♪ We reserve the right to delete any posts we feel are inappropriate or ones that become too dramatic. If you make an off-topic post, you will receive one warning. The second time you do it, you will be banned. If you feel you have been unfairly banned, you may be readmitted per a mod's discretion. If your account has been hacked and you post about shoes/sunglasses/other spam, you will be banned. The group admins are Abiba Champignon, Meghan Sanders, and Nicole Kathleen. Message any public mod if you have any questions.

After the invoice is PAID!! To ship items out and provide tracking number VIA Payapl. WEEKENDS &amp; HOLIDAYS dont count! If you cant get the item out within that time frame. Second time you will be Banned If you claim a item and leave a vaild email. You are commited to that purchase. You have 12 hrs to pay for that invoice. You fail to do so. First time you will be muted for 7 days Second time you will be BANNED!!! Sellers if the invoice is not paid within the time allowed.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 STITCH FIX Buy, Sell &amp; ISO Only!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for buying &amp; selling "NEW" Stitch Fix items, "EXCELLENT CONDITION" Stitch Fix items and for posting "ISO" ("In Search Of") Stitch Fix items that you've been dying to get. Please refrain from posting Stitch Fix items that are over 2 years old. We want to keep this group fresh with newer items. STITCH FIX items only. Items NOT from STITCH FIX will be deleted. Please DO NOT post old STITCH FIX items in this group. We want to keep this board to the NEWER items that you've been receiving in your more current fixes. Posts with very old items will be deleted. If the item is more than 2 years old, do not post it. NO "closet clean out" posts. Your post will be deleted. You can call your post "Items for Sale" or something along those lines. If you have multiple items for sale, make sure you post all the items/pictures in the main post. DO NOT post them in the comments. Refrain from posting more than 5 items in one post. We do not want the posts to get messy and overwhelmed with items. Please include a real life photo of your item along with the Stitch Fix style card or the Stitch Fix app pic of your item if you can. If your item is also posted on other boards, please write "CROSS POSTED" in the description. If other people are interested in the item on other boards, please communicate and make it known someone else has responded first on another board. We want to be as fair as possible when it comes to buying. If you are 100% sure you want to buy an item, please write "SOLD" and you can also include your PayPal email address so the buyer can go ahead and invoice you. If you don't feel comfortable leaving your email address on the post, then please PM the seller and let her know you sent her a PM in the post. If you want an item but have a question or two first, please write "SOLD PENDING QUESTION" and then ask what question it is you want answered. PAYMENT: PAYPAL ONLY! Please be considerate to buyers as they are most likely ready to checkout and are waiting for your money in their PayPal, so if you want to buy their item, pay them ASAP. If you change your mind, do not ignore them, just politely let them know you changed your mind. It is up to the buyer to hold the item for as long as they think is appropriate for you to pay them. Make sure to pay via PayPal Goods and Services, that way it is protected. PayPal Friends and Family is not protected. Once your item has been paid for by the buyer, please mark it as SOLD. Once the buyer has received the item, you can DELETE the post. ABSOLUTELY NO referral links allowed. You will be deleted and blocked from the group. NWT = New With Tags NWOT = New Without Tags EUC = Excellent Used Condition ISO = In Search Of 🦄 (unicorn emoji) = Your Must Have Item Administrators are not responsible for transactions, but please report any problems that might occur. Please be kind and respectful to everyone. NO DRAMA! Invite all your Stitch Fix friends!

                 This page is created for Carters, Oshkosh, old navy, gap, children's place and any other children's brands... pretty much any name brand clothing, shoes, accessories, etc. We all love stylish clothes but hate the prices... This is to help keep your child looking great without spending a fortune!! Please ONLY post these brands unless approved by admin!! NO DRAMA and always be fair!!! Have fun shopping! APPROVING POST: both admins work full time along with being full time mommies! We try to get to the post as soon as we can, please allow 24 hrs for post to be approved! If your post do not get approved in a timely manner please contact me or mandi Nichols. Please do not post duplicates, that only delays approving time! *BRANDS ALLOWED* Carters, Oshkosh, old navy, children's place, gap, Gymboree, mud pie, smocked outfits, giggle moon, La Jenna, peaches and cream, squeaky shoes, rare edition, Nike, under armour, and jumping bean. I'm not strict about brands just make sure that are nice name brand clothes. If there is a brand you have you can feel free to let me know and I will let you know if it's ok!! *POSTING AN ITEM FOR SALE* When posting something for sale, if ITS MORE THAN 1-2 items you're selling please post as a purge. Also add price, size, condition of the item on, smoke free/pet free or friendly home and location or if you are wanting to pay through PayPal. If someone comments wanting/ or asking a question an item they have 2 hours on a single selling item 1 hour on a purge or flash sale to let you know if they want it or not. If it's past that time move on to the next person. Also make sure when your item sells that you delete it. *PAYING THROUGH PAYPAL* If you comment on a post asking a question about an item Please be courteous to others and let them know if you want or pass. And if you post your PayPal first please pay within 24 hours of the person sending an invoice it gives others a chance to get it. Any non payer will be removed from the group. If you claim an item including PayPal you can not pass, you must pay. the only way to pass on an item is posting hold pending question and your question then whether or not pass or claim. *NEVER PAY FRIENDS/FAMILY* everything must be invoiced! *SHIPPING* If someone buys your item please make sure you get their item shipped out as soon as you can. We don't want scammers here. If an item is not shipped out 7-10 days after the invoice is paid unless discussed other wise, please contact admin once admin is contacted if the item is still not shipped you just file a claim on paypal! NON PAYER LIST: Chloe Edwards Comfort Martin

                 This page is for ALL brands, such as Old Navy, Gap, Mud-pie, Gymboree, Janie and Jack, Baby Ralph Lauren, Vans, Hurley and rare additions or accessories. purges are welcomed, and it's DRAMA FREE! Please note that all buyers should use their discretion when purchasing. We are not responsible for any transactions on this page. Please be respectful to all members at all times. Basic Rules and BST etiquette: Please post Nice items such as Gap, Mudpie, Janie and Jack, Naartjie, Matilda Jane, Mini Boden and Tea collection. If you have any doubts contact an admin. Please use Full descriptions of items. Smoking/non smoking homes, pet friendly or not plus condition. Disclose any ww, holes, stains, snags before the sale. Include the amount charging for shipping or state exact shipping will be added or is included in price. No price caps Flash sales and purge posts welcome, as well as auction posts and Deal or no deal posts, be sure to include all info to avoid confusion or disputes...each item should be numbered for easy reference. Claim with Sold in replies To claim an item put sold and your PayPal address. OR send pp address through a private message. Holds are up to the seller, please state how long holds are good for. Be reasonable or use at least the 24 hour rule. Please let the seller know if you have sent a message as it most likely will go to the "others" folder. Once you have stated sold you are committing to the sale. Do Not back out of sales. Please follow through or work out with the seller. It is Very rude to back out of sales. You may be Removed from the page for this. 24 hours to invoice and 48 to ship is standard. If something is holding this timeline up please communicate!!! No preorders, all items must be ready to ship. No outside advertisements this just clogs up the feed and makes it difficult to see the sale posts. First to post sold is winner... holds for questions are kind... This site is very drama free and we quite enjoy that! If there are continued issues we will be forced to block those causing issues to protect our members and group! No selling on other people's post!

                 The Locust&amp;WildHoney Community
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 📣UPDATE TO THE COMMUNITY📣 Going Forward, please abide by these Guidelines. If you have any questions we are all ears. 🙏🏼 First and Foremost, Welcome to the Locust and WildHoney Community! I’d like to thank you for taking the time to invest yourself in what we’re trying to accomplish through the channel, community and Facebook Group! Guidelines and Standards: BUYING - Make sure to always protect yourself and use third parties such as PayPal to secure a transaction. **We are not responsible for any transactions performed in the group or out. SELLING - All for sale post must have the following to be approved by a Mod. ⁃ Price ⁃ Tagged pic ⁃ Sizes ONLY AUTHENTIC GOODS. Anything sold falsely as an authentic good will result in being Banned. TRADING - There is no better way to perform a trade then to meet in person in a public location. However, for the majority of you all, this won’t be possible. Please, always take the extra measures before sending anything out. Legit check the person you are inquiring for a trade in the community. Use PayPal and buy/sell each others goods to make it a transaction. Or find a trusted middleman who can handle the trade. DISCUSSION - Discussions are the heartbeat of the community and we welcome all questions and opinions. It doesn’t always have to be fashion related as we all share different backgrounds. What we don’t welcome is use of aggressive and offensive language. We are a community that supports each other, any offensive language towards a fellow member will be warned. If inappropriate language continues, a soft Ban for 24 hours will be placed. If a 3rd strike should occur, Banishment from the community will follow. Prayer Requests are ALWAYS welcomed. PROMOTION - This is not a page for self promotion. Any post that are meant to further push a brand or media presence will be denied. We will have separate threads dedicated to sharing social media pages such as Instagram, YouTube, Snapchat etc. The Admins will try their best to monitor all activity in the group, but if you see something PLEASE REPORT IT. It will bring it to the front of our attention and we can act immediately to take care of any issues in the community. Well, now that the guidelines and standards are out the way. I look forward to having you in this community and learning more about you all. This is your house, have fun!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 PLEASE READ BEFORE POSTING Welcome to Anti Social Social Club Talk. This page is for the discussion, buying, selling and trading of Anti Social Club clothes. RULES: 1) All sale posts or comments (this includes comments) must include tagged pictures (of item in hand, confirmation emails do not suffice) including your Facebook name and a BIN price. "M here/I have one" etc. Needs a tagged picture and BIN. 2) Pictures and comments within the group should not be offensive ie. racist, homophobic or flaming 3) The page is for the discussion of Anti Social Social Club clothing only however if you wish to trade an item for assc clothing, you're more than welcome to. 4) Promoting your brand requires Admin approval. 5) Scamming of any kind is not tolerated and you will be banned from the group should you be found to be scamming. 6) Your post will be deleted by an admin should it breach any rules. The selling rules are there to prove product authenticity and ownership of the item. 7) Posts can only be bumped once every 12 hours. This is to keep the page useable. 8)Breaking the rules will result in a strike, three strikes and you will be banned. These are not hard rules to follow and it's only to ensure legit selling within the group. As this is an international group, it may be good to state where you are located when selling. If you have any questions, please contact an admin. **When buying, paying via Goods and Services through Paypal is highly recommended as it ensures both of the buyer and seller in the event of issues** This page is not in anyway officially affiliated with Anti Social Social Club and is simply a community group.                <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Elizabethan Costume
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 THESE ARE THE RULES. PLEASE READ &amp; ABIDE BY THEM. This group is for people fascinated with the clothing and fashions of the 16th century. Anything from the Tudor period (1485-1603) is fair game. Primary focus: England; secondary focus: worldwide. FINDING THINGS: We’ve amassed a vast repository of information since 2008. - Use the Search function to find past discussions. - Read through earlier threads before starting to post. - Use the documents in the Files section for answers to many basic questions, including where to buy. PICTURES: - Anyone may post images. - Label period images or details: WHEN, WHO, and the NAME of the ARTIST. This will help sort out the natural jumbling from years of postings. - DO NOT post links to Pinterest or other picture sites without adding labels or useful comments. - If you post multiple related pictures, group them in an album. NO SALES/ADVERTISING: - We maintain a well-grounded no-direct-sales-or-self-advertisement policy in this group. - The Files section contains documents with links to places to buy things. Please place vendor information there, not in the main feed. - Direct sales posts will be deleted, and repeat offenders may be removed from the group. SHARED FILES &amp; COPYRIGHTS: - Anyone may create documents or post files. - DO NOT add files of anything that is under copyright, unless you are the original author or have the explicit permission of the original author. - Same goes for patterns and original designs. HISTORICAL ACCURACY: While your Co-Mods and many group members delight in historicity, this group is specifically titled "Costume" with all the variants that wonderful word implies. There is no "right" way to approach the subject, so tolerance is the watchword. Our members come to this subject with many different goals, from 110% historical accuracy, to trying to put together something to wear to a Renn Faire in a carpark. And that’s just fine. Try to stick to the 1485-1603 period, but be tolerant. TONE: - Be nice. Our motto is “Points Sans Petitesse,” meaning “Stitchery Without Bitchery.” - DO NOT say something about anyone – ECBee or not -- unless you’d say it to their face in a room full of mutual friends. This applies to costumers, painters, historians, curators, seamsters, actors, etc. - Even if you *are* the type of person would say snarky things to someone's face, don't do it here. - Respect, civility, and kindness are required. Playfulness and supportiveness are encouraged. THE CO-MODS: - If you have a problem with something someone says in a thread, don’t flame. Contact one of the Co-Mods and discuss it reasonably. Don’t propagate bad manners. - EC is not a democracy. Membership is largely predicated on behavior. If what you're doing is offensive to any of the three Co-Mods, you'll be removed from the group, sometimes after a warning, sometimes not. As Benevolent Despots we're not required to justify our actions (or moods) to anyone but ourselves.
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This page is for Buying, Selling and Trading (BST) of new and gently used cabi clothing only. This site is not operated, managed or operated by CAbi in any way shape or form Listing your items - YOU MUST LIST YOUR ITEMS INDIVIDUALLY!!! EACH ITEM MUST HAVE its OWN POST AND MUST CONTAIN: EACH ITEM MUST HAVE its OWN POST! All items MUST have an IRL (in real life) picture. When posting, your post must include the following - Picture - Price (all prices must include shipping cost) - Condition Abbreviations for condition of items - NWT = New with tags NWOT = New without tags EUC = Excellent used condition VGUC = Very good used condition GUC = Good Used condition - Size 4. If you see something you are interested in - please mark interested. You can then follow up with a private message. Those must comment on the board to show interest (and sellers/buyers should go in order of who has posted on the board) - we then recommend sending a message privately to make arrangements. Please coordinate the details of all transactions and any negotiations privately - not on the board. We request that you mail your item in a timely fashion if you are the seller - 3-4 days is a good protocol to follow. We understand things come up but try to ship ASAP so the buyer can enjoy their item asap! You may post or bump a LIMIT of 10 items per 24 hours. That is a combined limit. Please do not post more than 10 items per 24 hours (new items or bumped items). Please do not piggyback on someone else's For Sale or ISO. If you have the same item in a different size, color, etc or are looking for the same item in a different size, please make your own listing. This keeps it fair for everyone. Please refrain from commenting on another's post that you are also looking for that item OR that you also have that item OR that you have that item in another color, size, etc OR that you... You get the idea! Even if the item runs BIG OR SMALL, please do not comment with another size. If you have something to sell differs from the ISO, please post your own sale listing. Tagging someone on a post does not create a place in line for buying an item. There is no holding of items out of fairness to all buyers on cabi Resale. The purchasing line begins with the first post made personally by an interested buyer. Happy Shopping! WE DO NOT ALLOW THE CURRENT CAbi LINE OF ITEMS TO BE SOLD ON THIS SITE - THIS IS ONLY FOR PAST SEASONS. NO soliciting or inviting anyone to your cabi team. This is strictly prohibited and you will be immediately removed from the site without notice. Your admins can be found by going to members/admins!- ADMIN TEAM *cabi representatives are not supposed to sell their seasonal items online per their rep agreement. We are not affiliated with cabi and we are not enforcing this - so if you are a rep you are selling at your own risk

                 TO NEW MEMBERS: A $4 contribution is required to join this group, this is a private group. EXISTING MEMBERS are not required to pay the $4 but donations would be greatly appreciated. NEW UPDATE: purges of more than 10 items per listing are not allowed. Post containing more than 10 items will be deleted. "ONLY LULULEMON OR IVIVVA CLOTHING ALLOWED"' OTHER POSTS WILL BE DELETED and MEMBERS WHO FAIL TO FOLLOW THIS RULE WILL BE PERMANENTLY Removed. No gift cards allowed to sell. Do not crowd the wall with multiple items (minimum 5 at a time) or make one single listing for all of them. This is a group to buy sell and trade Lululemon products. This is a drama free group so we advise you to be respectful to all the members please do not comment on anybody's price if you don't like the price move on. Members who do not follow this rule will be deleted. We strongly advise you do your transactions through Paypal not friends and family. make sure you get " as goods " request or an invoice. Do not hijack any body's sale post. Post your own item separately. If you would like to purchase an item indicate that you're interested or send the seller a personal message. Do not ask if item is still available unless you are interested or message seller asking if item is available and then disappear. (that is very rude). Also do not do iso posts and never respond to the people who took the time to comment and send you pictures and disappear. Be respectful and acknowledge the time people took to provide you with options to buy. (members will be removed it they do not comment on their own iso.. a thank you or pass will be enough) You are allowed to bump your items once every 24 hours. If you post in multiple sites make sure you write cross posted in your posts. MEMBERS WHO POST WANT,SOLD, INTERESTED. GET THE ITEM ( And must follow through with the sale ) Non payers will get blocked. Please report to administration. PMING YOU WANT THE ITEM IS NOT ALLOWED. 1. Don't post items unless you can ship in a timely manner. (non shippers get blocked from the group ) 2. If you find an issue with the item you purchased open a paypal claim. Be ready to provide pictures of the listing that can prove your claim. Make sure you have enough reasons to return. Not fitting in the item its not an excuse. 3.Also if you are interested in an item do not let the seller hanging and waiting for your paypal for days . That is very rude and you might get removed. 4.If you submit an offer please do it through the private messages. If the seller doesn't agree with the offer You must respect it and move on. Do leave rude comments for not accepting the offer. People who get reported doing so will be removed without warning. ✔️Template for your listing . ✔️name of item ,✔️ size ,✔️color, ✔️condition , ✔️shipping included or not? . ❓any other information if size is not available, provide some measurements. ●●●●New members must read the Rules before posting thanks ●●●●

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Vintage Clothing Fixes, Restorations, Alterations Etc. 1900-1960's
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for before and after photos of any fixes, alterations or restorations of vintage clothing from the 1900's-1960's. Please DO NOT post vintage dresses that have been "modernized" or "upcycled" as I will delete you for ruining vintage. This page is to give others ideas on how to fix their damaged vintage in an attempt to bring it back to it's original glory! Examples: Adding a gusset to armpits to give arm mobility. Removing ripped sleeves from a dress and giving thin straps or strapless. Fixing uneven hem on dress Taking an item in and out to fit you. Patching holes Reconstruction of item that is falling apart. Removing stains The point is to try and keep the item looking as close to the original as possible! Please only give advice on cleaning and repair methods that you have actually attempted yourself with success to avoid damaging the clothing further. If there is something that has damaged your items further, please let us know that as well! Look forward to seeing your photos! This group is NOT for: • Selling/Buying • Promoting your page or business • Asking for votes on competitions • Posting links to websites that have nothing to do with fixing vintage clothing All posts with any of the above will be deleted and multiple posts from one person will result in you being banned. Please be kind to each other!
                </div>

                 We're probably too intense for you. MODCLOTH FASHION CHAT GROUP: https://m.facebook.com/groups/232431440605748 Welcome to ModCloth BST! This is a Modcloth and similar styled clothing BST. ***We delete items that don't fall within the ModCloth style category***. We only have a few rules, so please abide by them. If your post is gone, you didn't abide by the rules: -NO Lularoe/LLR!! This also goes for an over saturation of department store brands; we allow minimal modcloth styled items, but this is not for target/old navy/torrid clothing. Our cover photo lays out the style! -No claiming prior to items being posted, you must wait until the seller has listed them before inquiring information. No teaser posts, as a seller, you need to post within 20 minutes of making a thread. -ONLY bump once every 24 (TWENTY-FOUR) hours. -US Shipping and fees MUST be included in your listing price! This is a US based group, so international prices are an additional amount; it's required to disclose if you're international. -NO drama. SAY IT WITH ME, nOOoO dRaMa -NO business ads or links! THIS INCLUDES ETSY, EBAY, POSHMARK, GO FUND MES, OTHER GROUPS AND SELLING PAGES. Pinterest boards are allowed but must have all information in the description. Handmade items are allowed RTS. -Sellers discretion to whom they sell to. Buyers are not obligated to purchase, but if you have 3 non-payments with no communication, you're removed. -All postings must be BST related - take chit chat to sister group. That's it! Yay! So easy. There is a feedback document, shipping guide AND shop our closet document under files; I recommend utilizing them. Thanks for joining and have a fabulous time! Don't hesitate to contact Becca Bowers or Kelsea Esparza with any questions, concerns, or issues.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Poshmark Thrifters
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Please enter your closet name in the space provided when you are requesting to join this group. We will not accept your request without this information. If your closet isn't currently selling we suggest you join our main Poshmark group until you get your closet up and running. www.facebook.com/groups/poshmark Guidelines and Rules: This is a Poshmark Thrifters Group. It is for anything related to thrifting on Poshmark only. If you have a question about another topic please post it in the main Poshmark group. You must have a Poshmark closet to be a member of this group. Need Pricing help – Post here! If you are out shopping and you are not sure what to buy, post a picture, we will give you our opinion if you should get it or not! Looking for a stock image? – let us see if we can help? Please provide pictures of all tags (including fabric content) and front and back of the item if you're looking for a stock picture. Are you in the know and want to help thrifters with their questions? Want to show us your Amazing haul? Let us see it! We love a bargain! Want to know what are good brands to buy, Ask us what we’ve sold lately! Rules: Thrifting Posts only! Once you have found the answer you are looking for, please delete or turn off the commenting for your post (arrow is in the top right hand corner, scroll down to Turn off commenting) Say Thank you if someone helps you! Please do not solicit shares in return for advice. However, you can ask someone who has helped you their closet name to follow/share their closet as thanks. Sharing is not required. No drama. Be respectful. Moderators have discretion in closing/deleting posts, giving warnings and removing members from the group for failure to follow the rules. No discussion of other selling platforms permitted - Poshmark only. Other platforms can only be mentioned as recommendations as better/faster/more profitable selling sites for a particular item in question. If you want to advertise your Thrifted bundle deals here, please post accordingly. All transactions need to go through Poshmark! Moderators: Anona Anonyuo @haithereblossm Olesya Zakharkina @gumlets Cassie Cruise @cruisecoutoure

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Delta Gamma Shirt Swap!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is meant to be a place where Delta Gamma members can swap shirts. PLEASE read all of the group's rules before posting: To join, you must answer the questions presented to you. Feel free to message an Admin if you've sent a request, answered questions and have not been able to access the group at least 3 business days after. All profiles are checked before admission to make sure you're not spam. This is not an official DG social media forum, but it will adhere to the standards of our sisterhood. If you post something that is not in line with our values, it will be deleted and you will be removed from the group. This group is NOT a place for T-shirt vendors to sell their product. If you post a shirt for sale, the post will be deleted. If you are an unlicensed vendor, you will be reported to Affinity Consultants for unlawful use of trademarks. Only DG members that are reps will be allowed in this group. No reps of other affiliations. If you are a DG member, you may post T-shirts and other DG items for trade or sale, but please remember the intent of the group is to swap shirts. If you have reason to believe a member is not a member of Delta Gamma, please contact one of the Admins of the page. Thank you!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Bailey's Blossoms BST
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Bailey's Blossoms "Buy, Sell, Trade" group! GROUP RULES: *By joining this group you are agreeing to abide by the rules below. Failure to follow them, will result in removal from the group.* -NO DRAMA! Kindness is key! -NO sales of items outside of Bailey's Blossoms branded clothing and accessories. -PHOTOS: Please do not use stock photos. Members would like to see photos of the actual item you are selling. -SOLD: Once your item is SOLD, please DELETE IT. - We ask our Wholesale Partners to post on the Wholesale BST page. Posts from Wholesale or Resale Partners (those reselling in mass quantities) will not be approved. -PRICE/DESCRIPTION: Please list a PRICE or TRADE along with general descriptions and location of your item(s). If there is no PRICE, your ad will be deleted. Once listed, seller CANNOT raise the price. -NO SHARING OF ADS FROM OTHER GROUPS/PAGES -NO FUNDRAISING SALES. -NO Soliciting for donations. -ORDER OF COMMENTS: ALWAYS go in order of the comments. PM's (personal messages) without a comment on the post do not count as a place in line. TAGGING another member does not place that person in line. MBI (might be interested).. is NOT a place in line. ASKING A QUESTION is showing interest and puts said person in line for that item. Sellers are under no obligation to hold an item for a period of time (example 4-5 days, or until a buyers next pay). -Make sure you have the money to purchase before commenting and placing yourself in line. **PAYMENTS &amp; SHIPMENT - buyers have 24hours to submit payment via PayPal, before seller will move to the next person in line. Sellers have 48hrs to ship the item and provide tracking to the buyer. Please do NOT ship any item prior to payment being collected. -NO COMMENTS ON ANY ITEM... UNLESS YOU HAVE INTEREST IN PURCHASING THAT ITEM. No comment about pricing, getting it somewhere else cheaper, priced too low or priced too high. -ALL SALES ARE FINAL - if there is an issue with your items upon receipt, please contact the seller directly. -Poaching or Snaking a sale: If someone has an item for sale and you have the same or similar item.. DO NOT post on their item that you have one for sale or that yours is cheaper and or available. -Swearing and foul language is not tolerated. -NO RANTING or bashing other members. This is a friendly space please! If you have a problem with a member please private message the person or an admin. This group is not affiliated with Bailey's Blossoms, LLC, and its admins &amp; Facebook are not responsible for transactions that happen in the group - buy, sell &amp; trade at your own risk. The creator and administrators of this group reserve the right to refuse, reject, or terminate any member or prospective member of this group.                  Costume People
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This page is for film theatre and academic PROFESSIONAL costume designers and artisans. It is designed as a place to share information, resources and discussions for professional theatrical theatre, film, television and academic costume designers and supporting artisans. This page IS NOT intended as a forum for those most interested in the Cosplay/gaming /role-play arena, or Renaissance fair or in "halloween" costumes--both commercial or home made. It is. however, designed for those with an interest in the costume industry as practiced in a professional venue. Members are encouraged to provide links to articles and useful websites as well as links to their personal costume related business. Questions comments and costume chatter are welcome. But we ask members to be supportive and respectful of the work of others. Posts for merchandise not related to the intent of this page will be deleted and posters will be blocked. Job posts are welcome--both for long and short term positions. We ask that the job poster reference a salary/rate if it is known, or to acknowledge that the salary is not known. The intent of this page is to be a supportive resource and forum for those working in the industry.

                 DUE TO THE VOLUME OF REQUESTS WE GET, WE CAN NOT LOOK FOR INDIVIDUAL REQUESTS SO PLEASE DON'T ASK US TO. If you don't answer the questions that form part of the request process, or your profile doesn't meet the requirements outlined below, your request will automatically be deleted. WE ASK THAT YOU ANSWER ALL THREE OF THE QUESTIONS WE HAVE INCLUDED WHEN YOU SUBMIT YOUR REQUEST TO JOIN THE GROUP AND THAT YOU PLEASE HAVE YOUR FRIENDS LIST AND THE PAGES YOU HAVE LIKED VISIBLE. If you can’t change your settings for work or safety issues, that’s fine, we are happy to work with you to find an alternative :) Just send a PM to Beatrice Smith and she'll help you out. However, if you refuse to work with the admin team, are rude in response to our requests for extra information or feel affronted by our requirements, this probably isn’t the group for you :) We ask for the same things from everyone who requests to join the group. Our duty is to the safety and security our members, the requirements we have in place and your interaction with us while we work to add you to the group are the best indicators that we have to see if you are a good fit for our group :) The more information we can see the faster you will be accepted. If you are having issues being accepted into the group it will be because your privacy settings are too high, your Friends List and Like Segments are not visible, and/or you haven't answered the membership questions. We don't look for photos of you in your BM, and we aren't looking to pry into your private lives, we are just trying to make sure that all the requests we accept are from legitimate BM Fans and not spambots, Boutiques, eBay Resellers and people who are joining to ask you for photos of you in your BM. We want to keep you as safe as possible from scammers and predators. Once you have joined the group , please make sure you read "this is how we roll" doc and "limited / banned items" doc and the pinned post for the guidelines on how the page works before you post or comment. The BMC BSS Admin Team

                 Welcome to Eve &amp; Mae Boutique!! We specialize in boutique clothing, athletic wear, jewelry, shoes, handbags, ect… at amazing, affordable prices! Our sizes range from S-3X! Find us on Instagram @lisagraffstyle. New product arrives daily so make sure to turn on those notifications and text eve&amp;mae to 31996 to be the first to know about any amazing sales/product arrivals! Return Policy: Items can be returned for an online store credit only. All Items must be returned within 14 days after your order was delivered/received. If shipping back, it must be postdated on or before the 14th day. Return shipping is nonrefundable, unless there was a mistake on our end. Items must have original tags (if tags are not present it will need original packaging) be unwashed and unworn. Anything purchased at a discounted price is FINAL SALE and is not eligible for return or exchange! This includes Doorbuster items, Grab Bags, Accessories, or anything posted as ON SALE! Please allow our team 5-7 business days to process your return once it is received at our warehouse. Items that are returned to us after 14 days will not be accepted and your account will not be credited nor will it be shipped back to you. Your item will be forfeited and donated to a local shelter. If your item is damaged we need to hear from you by email (eveandmaeboutique@gmail.com) within 48 hours of receiving. Damaged items will be assessed by our team and a credit will be given to one of your accounts (credit card/store account credit) at our discretion. Shipping: Your item will ship within 3 business days of purchase! FREE shipping on orders paid within 1 hour of commenting. Shipping charges are subject to change at any time* If you are local pick up is welcome Once your package has been fulfilled and you have received tracking information from us, this means your package is now in the hands of the post office, USPS, and we are no longer liable. Store hours: Mon-Friday 9am-4pm MST Local Order Pickup Tuesday/Thursday 10am-12pm Any questions or concerns please email eveandmaeboutique@gmail.com Please allow up to 24-48 hours for a response to email. Due to the size of our group, we cannot respond to private messages or wall posts. Please direct your questions and/or concerns to eveandmaeboutique@gmail.com Thank you for your understanding! We appreciate when you add your friends or share our page on your newsfeed! We also love when you send pictures of you in your Eve &amp; Mae Outfits!!! Thank you for supporting our family business! xoxo

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Used Ren Faire Garb
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 A place for all rennies in Southern California areas to sell ren faire related garb and items to others! RULES: 1) All seller posts MUST have the following: An image of the item for sale, description, asking price, item location, and payment/shipping details. 2) Seller is responsible for removing post after the item has sold. 3) Should more than one person be interested in an item for sale, it is solely up to the seller to chose whom they wish to sell to, including if they wish to offer it to those interested at a higher price (aka change it to bidding). Please do this via PRIVATE MESSAGING so that we do not break into arguments of any kind in the comments of an item being sold. 4) BUY AT YOUR OWN RISK! Use paypal online which is pretty safe, or meet up in person to buy the item. Don't do mailed money order or cash transactions, which are usually pretty scammy. Any problems you may have with an item being sold here is strictly between the buyer and the seller and needs to be worked out between you two via private message or other contact. 5) No slandering or news posts of any kind. This is a place to sell your garb. We do not welcome drama, advertising, or anything unrelated to selling off our used items. 6) And on that note....used items only please! This is not a group for merchants to come and sell their wares. 7) Have fun! This group is just a way for us to help easily sell off or trade some of our items we no longer use. Anybody causing drama or is found to be scamming of any kind will be removed immediately from the group. Play nice everyone! :)

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Tiki-Tastic Art &amp; Fashion
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Ahola, Hulagals and Hulaguys! Welcome to Tiki-Tastic Art &amp; Fashion Page! "Tiki Tastic Art &amp; Fashion" is for people to post items for sell or trade or just cool Tiki things you see out in the world. This page is limited to strictly Tiki Style stuff, from clothing, jewelry, art, furniture to really anything Tiki related. Please only post items that you are selling, trading, seeking OR inspire you. This page is not for events, bands, blogs, podcasts, websites unless the event is specifically selling Tiki related items. Here are a few guidelines and rules to make sure everyone has a great experience. 1. Photos &amp; Description - Post a photo AND description of the product you are selling. It is important to note WHY this item is relevant to the "Tiki-Tastic Art &amp; Fashion page". Overall PLEASE include information so that people can stay ON the group and have all the info they need. People do not want to click out of the group! If your post is forwarded from another FB page or etsy/instagram/ebay with no context as to why it was posted to this group it WILL be deleted. 2. Bumping - there is a 3 bump rule as it's not fair to bump over and over again as moves other posts down the page. 3. First come first served - first person to comment "interested" on a item is 'first in line' the 2nd person is 2nd in line and so on and so forth, however if a seller has linked to a item they are selling on eBay or etsy then please be aware that 'buy it now' is outside of this page control. Also if the person first in line can't pay right away and the seller isn't happy to hold it for a few days or so on seller has full rights to go to next in line. All people that join the 'queue' must be in comment form none of this 'oh someone just pm me'. 4. Deleting - please take down your sold items as it's heartbreaking for everyone to find a great item then find out it's already sold and also it clogs up the page. 5. No Teasing - We do not allow teaser posts of items you hope or plan to sell someday as there is no way to validate these items will become a reality and distracts from those who have product to sell or trade. 6. Payment - we suggest you only send money via paypal and please do not send as gift. 7. Postage - use a tracking number so that the buyer and seller can track the item if needed. 8. Banning - we do keep a list of disreputable sellers/buyers and if needed people will be removed and banned . And no blocking of any Admins. 9. Be Polite - Please be mindful of being polite and friendly with others. We have a no cyberbullying policy. Keep in mind there is no emotion in text and come sometimes be taken in the wrong way so please think of this when leaving comments. Thank you for taking the time to read the rules and hope you enjoy the Tiki-Tastik Art &amp; Fashion Page!
                </div>

                 Tznius Modest Clothing Internet Finds
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 You must answer the group questions in order to be added to the group. As a Jewish woman, I find it very important to wear clothing that fit me. To me, that means finding something with appropriate hemlines and coverage that also makes me feel either beautiful or comfortable, depending on the occasion. This group has become the single forum on the Internet to discuss tznius clothes - how they fit, customer service, returns, etc. This is a very active group ranging from reviews to ISOs to advertisements. But be aware that this group is strictly for the purpose of discussing modest clothes. This group is open to any women interested in dressing modestly, whatever your religion or background. It is important to remember in your interactions in the group that there are many women here from different walks of life. This group is associated with the Instagram here: https://www.instagram.com/modestclothesaremything/

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Modern Pinups
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 READ BEFORE APPLYING FOR MEMBERSHIP. We're a style advice &amp; general discussion group for modern pinups. If you personally wear pinup-style clothing you are welcome here. We were founded as PUG Style Pinups, the Facebook home of the PUG Style crew from PinupGirlStyle.com. Since PUG later started their own official group, we have since expanded to be a general discussion group for all pinup lovers and all pinup brands, and the new name Modern Pinups reflects that. Buying, selling, or in search of clothes? Please use one of the many swap/sell groups. Questions for PUG staff? Please use the Pinup Girl Clothing Customer Lounge. Questions for Micheline Pitt? Please use The Vixen's Lounge. Membership here is limited to people who personally wear pinup style clothing (or aspire to). This group explicitly includes trans &amp; gender-variant people and men as long as they personally wear the clothing. If you personally wear pinup and get rejected for membership, please send a message stating your interest in pinup to one of the admins. Finally, the members of this group believe that pinup is for everyone - from those of us who dress in full 1950s vintage repro every day to people who own just a few pieces. We are committed to diversity and inclusion. PS: While the mods do our best, we're volunteers and checking out potential members can take a while. The best way to fast-track yourself is to send the mods a message or change your profile photo or cover photo to something that clearly reflects your interest in pinup style.

                 ✨ Link us!: https://facebook.com/groups/japanesefashion ❤️ Have fashion news to share or promote? Try submitting a post! http://dokipress.com/submit ✨ Come join the J-Fashion fun! Feel free to add your friends to the group! ✨ ✨ This group is primarily based in California, United States, but members from all over the world are welcome! ✨ ✨ When you join, please introduce yourself! ✨ ❤️ You can sell in this group, but buyers beware we are not responsible for any transaction problems! ❤️ We accept all and any types of Japanese Fashion styles, from Decora, Lolita, Larme Kei, Fairy Kei, Pastel Goth, Gothic Lolita, Street Style to even high Japanese fashion! Whether you're a casual fashionista, a die-hard J-fashion maniac, the J-Fashion group welcomes you! ⚠ Rules &amp; Goals: 1. Please welcome other members to the group and be accepting of the values and opinions of those who post and comment! 2. Discuss and connect with J-Fashion fans from all over the world! 3. Have fun with local meetups, event gatherings, and more! ⚠ Posting Rule: Please add some context such as a excerpt, description, or caption for any relevant articles that you share under your post. Our goal is to facilitate discussion on J-fashion and J-culture, not to simply share or market articles. ⚠ Rules on posting: 1. Posts about all J-fashion styles are allowed. Decora, Lolita, Larme Kei, Fairy Kei, Street Style and more! We're here to promote and learn about different groups! 2. Off-topic posts are okay, just be courteous to other members. 3. If you would like to posts items for sale, that is okay too, but keep in mind that there are other Facebook groups and online communities where that is their primary purpose. 4. Please be respectful of other members. This group is meant to be global and diverse. Discussion is naturally going to get heated, but do not be offensive to other members of this group. 5. All posts are subject to removal by admins if deemed inappropriate.
